1b1(phal chen): 'phags pa sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba/bam po drug cu
1b2(phal chen): rtsa gsum pa/de nas byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs chen po de'i nang nas/byang
1b3(phal chen): chub sems dpa' kha cig 'di snyam du sems te/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
1b4(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing na ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/sangs
2a1(phal chen): /rgyus bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang /'byung ba rnam par dag pa ni ji
2a2(phal chen): tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/sangs rgyas bco mi ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung ni
2a3(phal chen): ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mau khyab/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas skye ba ni ji tsam zhig
2a4(phal chen): tu bsam gyis mi khyab/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhini gshegs po'i sku ni ji tsam zhig tu
2a5(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyabo/sangs rgyaso bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig tu
2b1(phal chen): s+yas rgyas bcom ldan dus rnams kyi de bzhin ga shegs pa'i rnam ra 'phrul ni dzin+dam+b+ha nA k+sha t+yA sam gyis mi khyu/sang sa rgyas
2b2(phal chen): bcom ldan sa rnames kyi tshogs pa mi me 'bri rnam par spyod pa ni dz+nyAnam chog tu bsam gyis mi khyab/sangs rgyas bcom ldan
2b3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sa sa rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa ni ji tshim zhig hU~M bsam gyis me khye snum pa dang /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi
2b4(phal chen): sems da 'di dag gi sems thugasagis thugs chu nas/byung chub sems de ut+pala'i snang /sangs rgya
2b5(phal chen): sa kyis byin tu 'jug/sa sa rgyas kyi mi shes tu rkyen dang ldan par mdzad//de 'dzin pa shegs pa
3a1(phal chen): /kyis snang bar mdzad do//soms rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis yongs su rgyas par mdzad do//sangs rgyas
3a2(phal chen): kyi mi 'jig pa la rab tu bzhag gi/sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa khong du chud par mdzad do//sangs rgyas kyi bdag
3a3(phal chen): nyid che ba nyid dang /rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do//chags pa med pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go/
3a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad ga cig nas gcig tu rgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs par mdzad do//sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod
3a5(phal chen): du med pa la rab tu bzhag pa mdzad do//de nas byang chub sems dpa' ut+pa la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa rig cing
3a6(phal chen): khong du chud pas/chags pa med pa'i dbyings su bsgrubs pa'i yid dang /chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par gnas
3b1(phal chen): pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i sangs
3b2(phal chen): rgyas blta ba dang /snying rje chen pos lta ba'i sems can thams cad yongasu sbyongs pa'i go cha chen po dang /byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam dang /spyod pa'i
3b3(phal chen): dkyil 'khor rgyun chad pa med pa dang /sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par sgrub pa skad cig gi cha shas la rnam par spyod pa dang /thams cad mkhyen
3b4(phal chen): pa nyid kyi sgo mthong ba mi zad pa dang /tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i rnam pa/gzungs thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi
3b5(phal chen): mthus byang chub sems dpa' pad+mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smraso//kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom lnga ni 'das rnams ni tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa
3b6(phal chen): ste/kyi rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul po chen po la rnam par spyod pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom
3b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la sku'i mtshan nyid thams cad rab tu brnyes pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
4a1(phal chen): /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni ting nge 'dzin dang dgongs pas sbyar ba'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tha dad pa yang
4a2(phal chen): dag par mkhyen pa bzhi ni brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu ston pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/sangs rgyas kyi chos thams
4a3(phal chen): cad la byas mo gyis mi khyab par rnam par spyod pa'o//sangs rgyas bco ma ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o//sangs
4a4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings thugasu chud po ni brjod du med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi
4a5(phal chen): mothu phyung ba ni/thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgya so bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugasu chud
4a6(phal chen): cing bstan pa ni bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'o//kye rgyal po'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings
4a7(phal chen): mtha' ding bung med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam pa bcu ste/bcu gang zhin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gzugs kyi sku rnam par dag pa ni
4b1(phal chen): rlu ma rna sa nga chu bas smrang ba yod nga na//byas na ma na dus sa mags dun na/chos pas nga ma pa na
4b2(phal chen): mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i snyani/'gro ba thams cad kyi sgra bsgribs pa med
4b3(phal chen): par thug su chud pas mtha' dang dbyung med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni/sangs rgyas kyi mnga' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
4b4(phal chen): brnyes pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljags shin tu yangs pa ni/chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gsung gi dbyangs rje su 'gro
4b5(phal chen): bas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i chos nyid ni sems can thams cad mo lus pa'i sems kyi rnam pa de bzhin ga shegs
4b6(phal chen): pa mthong ba rnam par dmigs pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi phrin las ni/chos kyi sku dang tha mi dad cing /dus gsum
4b7(phal chen): chags pa med par thugasu chud cing rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa bsgribs pa mi mnga' ba la
5a1(phal chen): rnam par spyod pa ni/sangs rgyas kyi gro 'phang dang /rnam par 'phrul ba dang /cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dpung med
5a2(phal chen): pa'o/rgyu sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/brjod du med pa'i rgyun byin gyis brlabs pas/sangs
5a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs po med pa yang dag par bstan te/bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmyigs par mdzad pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o//sbyangs
5a4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang /smon lam thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa ni/rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos
5a5(phal chen): yongasu rdzogs te/chos thams cad rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dpung med pa ste/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
5a6(phal chen): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnamaso//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni//
5a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig gcig la ye shes kyis mngon par bsgrubs pa yang dag par bstan pa'o//bcu gang zhe na/skad
5b1(phal chen): cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dga' ldan gyis granas nas 'pho ba yongs su bstan pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
5b2(phal chen): du byang chub sems dpa'i tshe yongs su bstan pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba yongasu bstan+da pa dang /skad cigs/
5b3(phal chen): gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs shing mngon par ra tshang brgya pa yongasu bstan pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi
5b4(phal chen): khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongasu bstan pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongasu smin
5b5(phal chen): nga'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du dus la brub par shes pas/sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba yongasu bstan pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams
5b6(phal chen): cad du sems can ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa brdud du med pa dang /sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmig sde pa yongasu bstun
5b7(phal chen): pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyan sna tshogs dang /rgyan brjod du med pa si de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu/
6a1(phal chen): phyung ba dang /thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongasu bstun pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnams bdag pa gcig ma
6a2(phal chen): yin pa thams cad yang su bstan pa dang /skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang /ma byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba zam
6a3(phal chen): cad du dbang po dang /brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dad byung ba dang /mos pa dang /sgyed pA na tha dad pa byung ba la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongasu postun pa ste
6a4(phal chen): gyi rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig pa ye shes mngon par sgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sgras
6a5(phal chen): po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'dra' ste/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni de'i/
6a6(phal chen): dus las mi 'da' bsnga dus su bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam da' smin pa dang /rnam par ma smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da'
6a7(phal chen): bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongasu snang ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa ni/de'i dus las na 'da' bas dus la
6b1(phal chen): bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud du cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs
6b2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhi ni du sku yongs su bstan pa ni dus las me 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs rgyas
6b3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams btang snyomasu bzhugs pa ni/de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang grong dang grong
6b4(phal chen): rdal du gshegs pa ni/de'i dus la ma 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongasu
6b5(phal chen): 'dzin pa ni/de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la
6b6(phal chen): gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dra rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis
6b7(phal chen): mi khyab pas rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa de'i dus rnam 'da' bas dus la ba'i pa yi// rgyal ba sras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba'o///
7a1(phal chen): kye rgyu la ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyu sna bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mu khyab ste/bcu
7a2(phal chen): gang zhe na/'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skyil mo dkrung gcig gis rgyas par dgong ba dang /dus gcig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yong su bstan
7a3(phal chen): pa dang /'od zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams mA lus pa thams cad snang bar bya ba dang /sku gzugs gcig gi lus dang /gzugs thams cad yongasu bstan
7a4(phal chen): pa dang /gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad mi lus par byin pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang /ye shes gcig rtogs pas chos thams cad
7a5(phal chen): la bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang /thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang /sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad
7a6(phal chen): med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang /dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ga 'phang gis rgyas par 'grengs pa dang /
7a7(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad dang ma 'dras par bzhugs shing /'das pa dang /ma byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis
7b1(phal chen): rgyud kyi tshul gyi gcig pa ste/kye rgyu la ba'i sgras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyasu bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o//kye rgyas
7b2(phal chen): bo'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/bcu gang zhe na 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams
7b3(phal chen): cad la 'jug pas/smon lam mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /lus med pa la lus mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /chos thams cad mi gnyis pa la mngon par 'tshang
7b4(phal chen): rgya ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /se mas can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa la sems can la dul ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /chos thams cad mtshan ma
7b5(phal chen): med pa la/mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'du ba dang /'jig pa mngon par
7b6(phal chen): sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /yul thams cad mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /chos thams cad brjod du med pa la chos
7b7(phal chen): kyi dbyingasu gsung mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /chos thams cad kun nas nyon mongs pa dang /rnam par byang chub 'jug pa med pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang /rnam par
8a1(phal chen): /byung du mngon pa sgrub pa'i ye shes dang /nus thams cad ma smos pa la skye ba dang /lkog tu'i mtshan ni/na ni 'brel par 'byung ba mngon par smra
8a2(phal chen): yA sheswA to/rgyal po sras bcu pa da nga gen+d+he/de bzhin gshegs pa rnams sangs rgyas kyi mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes so//sar+g+haM la bu'i sras pacu
8a3(phal chen): pa 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chud med pa'i khangasu chud pa dag ste/ ga non/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'asan sma ni sags
8a4(phal chen): cad kyi rjes 'byung ba'i khong su chud pa yin/sa rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul par mdzad pa ni/tshe'i la chen po gsum gyi khongs chud
8a5(phal chen): pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad lnga mkhas pa ni/spangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khangasu chud pa yin/
8a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyas rgyal ba ma s+t+rai dA dA ni/de bzhin ga shegs d+ma'i thang pa yang dag par mi khyen pa N+Di khengs bi yin/
8a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan la ma rnams sems can thams cid yang suM mi ga ting be ni/bru~M sa chen pa 'i khong rmed pa 'in/seM sa rgyas bcom ldan 'di sa rnam sa tu/
8b1(phal chen): mnyam par bzhug pa ni/dus thams cad du sems can thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i khongasu chud pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
8b2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba ni/sems can rnam par gdul ba thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa ni chos kyi
8b3(phal chen): dbyings thams cad khengasu chud pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi skad cig gcig tu ni 'das pa dang /ma byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye
8b4(phal chen): pa thams cad khongasu chud pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nyi ma gcig tu ni/dus gsum gyi bskal po'i grangs khongasu chud par bstan pa thams
8b5(phal chen): cad khongasu chud pa yin/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongasu chud pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di
8b6(phal chen): dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par bka' ba rnams te/bcu gang zhe na/bdud kyi dkrugs mA rab tu 'joms zhing rnam par
8b7(phal chen): 'thar pa ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//mu stegs can gzhan dang /phas kyi rgol ba tshar bcad pa ni/
9a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgyu che bya'i chos bzod par dka' dwa'o//'dul ba'i sems can tham+b+has ts+tshang+ga rab tu tshim par ma dzad pa
9a2(phal chen): ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che b+h+yo'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams
9a3(phal chen): cad du gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//chos kyi dbyings thugasu chud pa'i ye shes ni/
9a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skus khyab cing /sangs rgyas
9a5(phal chen): kyi sku rnam par phye ba ste tshogs thams cad du mi gnyis pa ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//gsung
9a6(phal chen): gri yan lag thoms cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang /thos par bya ba dang /gdul bar bya ba don yod par tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa
9a7(phal chen): med pas bstan pa'i tshul du tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi 'byung ba ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka'
9b1(phal chen): ba'o//snangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ba spu'i bu ga gcig nas/de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba skyed na/
9b2(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab cing thogs pa med pa'i tshul du'ijig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing /de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyis
9b3(phal chen): sku'i ba spu'i zu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
9b4(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba skyed yongasu ston cing /sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang /rang bzhin gyi
9b5(phal chen): lnga ba lbub dang /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing /sems can rnam par 'dul ba thogs pa med la 'jig rten gyi khas de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang mi bde ba dang
9b6(phal chen): gnod pa med kyang rdul shin tu phra ba de yang yangs par ma byas/'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chung bar ma byas par ji ltar granas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thug su chud pa'i ye shes mang
9b7(phal chen): ba ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/sangs rgyas
10a1(phal chen): kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la/sems can pha rol skye bsgribs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas par stsol na/de la bcom ldan 'das
10a2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos la bzod par dka' ba ste/kye rgyal ba'i sgras bcu po de dag ni/
10a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dradas kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che
10a4(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad du/kha na ma tho ba med cing /shin tu dag pa ste/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag par bsgrubs pa bdag nyid che ba ni/sngon
10a5(phal chen): gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du khan ma the ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang /me byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i sangs
10a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi rgyud du rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam par dag papa/rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma thob med cing shin tu rnam
10a7(phal chen): par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa ste/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ni/phyi ma'i ma
10b1(phal chen): myur thugs par gnas pas/rnam pa thams cad du kha nam tho ba mad cing shin tu rnam par dgu pa'o//sang+yas rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus gsum la mi gnas par rnam pa
10b2(phal chen): spyod cing chos thams cad la rten pa yang dag par bcom pas/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu
10b3(phal chen): rnam par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa la rnam par gzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10b4(phal chen): rnams kyi de dag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam ni sngon gyi mtha' dang /phyi ma'i mther chos
10b5(phal chen): kyi dbyings la gnas pas mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas/mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni//
10b6(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang /kha dog mthu' yas pas/'jig rten gyi
10b7(phal chen): khams thams cad na/sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par bzhugs pas/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa tha
11a1(phal chen): kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi brnyes pas bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar bzhugs///
11a2(phal chen): shing khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ro 'byin te/rgol ba'i nang na stag lta bu'i mthu dang ldan la/chos thams cad bstan pa la thugs sgron ma lta bu mnga' bas/sangs
11a3(phal chen): rgyas pocom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa thams cad du kha na mA tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//srungs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
11a4(phal chen): yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang mtshon gyi tshig thos pa tsam gyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems
11a5(phal chen): can rnams kyi yon shin tu sbyong zhing /mya ngan las 'das nas de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang /sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon zad par mi 'gyur bas/sangs
11a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi kham
11a7(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs shing /'jig rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na bzhugs kyang /'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pa'i sems can
11b1(phal chen): rnams kyis rdo su dran par byas na/sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing /
11b2(phal chen): shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/kye rgya le ba'i sgras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/rnam pa thams cad kha nu ma tho ba med
11b3(phal chen): cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas
11b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag pa la/sngon gyi smon lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan
11b5(phal chen): 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs
11b6(phal chen): pa sel bas/shin tu rnam par drug pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/sangs rgyas
11b7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rigs rnam par dag pas/shin tu rnam par dag
12a1(phal chen): /pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pa rnam par dag pas/shin tu rnam par dag pa yin//
12a2(phal chen): sangs rgya sa bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/chos kyi sku rlirig pa med pas/shin+da tu rnam par dge po yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad
12a3(phal chen): mkhyen po'i ye shes kyi phyung ba'i sgribs pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/sangs rgyas kyi rnam par
12a4(phal chen): zar pa thams cad la mthu chen pA brnyes shing /pa ri l-i phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu rnam par dge pa yin te/rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa de dag ni
12a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//kyi rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa
12a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad dru gnas pa ste/bcug shi na/sangs rgyasan su dran pa'i thob pa'i sems can rnams la dus thams
12a7(phal chen): cang du/sangs rgyas bstan pa da /sems can sems cad shes dang ldan pa rnams la/dus thams cad du chos bsten pa dang /sems can sangs rgyas la du bar
12b1(phal chen): sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dus thams cad du bskyed pa dang /chos kyi skyon med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang /'gro ba thams
12b2(phal chen): cad du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa dus thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang //de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dus thams cad du chags pa mi mnga' bar gshen
12b3(phal chen): ba dang /sems can thams cad la thugs rje chen po dus thams cad du mi gtong ba dang /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs
12b4(phal chen): pa med pa dang /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
12b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad du 'byung ba ste/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa/'jig rten gyi
12b6(phal chen): khams thams cad du 'byung zhing /dus thams cad du gnas pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
12b7(phal chen): rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams ste/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//
13a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med po brnyas pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
13a2(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi yul mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho ma zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa/bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga'
13a3(phal chen): bas ye shes rgya mchi mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/chos kyi char mngon par 'bebs pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan/
13a4(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang /legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyasra bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha'i thaMd
13a5(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyab par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mthe'i mur 'gro ba thams cad sangs rgyas
13a6(phal chen): kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par bsgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems
13a7(phal chen): dang spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi non pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi
13b1(phal chen): zad pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras
13b2(phal chen): bcu po 'dri dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te/bcu grang zhe na/'di lta ste/pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par
13b3(phal chen): byang ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di lta ste/chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang ma mnga' ba 'di ni /ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan
13b4(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di lta ste/thams cad kyang thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di lta ste/tha~Md
13b5(phal chen): kyang stobs bcu tshad med pa dang ldan pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di lta ste/thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu
13b6(phal chen): bskor ba 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di lta ste/thams cad kyang sems can 'dul ba yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas
13b7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di lta ste/thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
14a1(phal chen): kyi tshul yin n+do//'di lta ste/'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul
14a2(phal chen): yin no//'di lta ste/mi gnyis par yang dag par spyod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//'di
14a3(phal chen): lta ste ji ltar yongasu smin par gyur pa dang /dul bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la/sangs rgyas kyi yul mu mod pas/sangs rgyas kyi yongasu mya ngan las 'dra'
14a4(phal chen): ba ston pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin te/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
14a5(phal chen): tshul lo//kye rgyal ba'i sgras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcos rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas
14a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin
14a7(phal chen): tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang /rnam par smin pa shin tu bstan po'i sgor mtha' yas
14b1(phal chen): pa//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams dag dang /man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas
14b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can mtha' yas pa rnam par spyod pa'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems
14b3(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams ngag dang /man ngag gri so yongasu gzhog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems
14b4(phal chen): dpa'i khyod par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dra rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
14b5(phal chen): ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang /'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub
14b6(phal chen): sems dpa'i bsam pa dang /mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yong su bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams
14b7(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad du 'das pa dang /ma byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing
15a1(phal chen): brjod pa dang /yongs su bshad pas/sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de
15a2(phal chen): dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas
15a3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub pa ste/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongasu
15a4(phal chen): bstan pa ni/sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi
15a5(phal chen): phrin las sgrub po//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po//sangs rgyas
15a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po//sa dang /chu dang /me dang rlung gis kyang /sangs
15a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po//sangs rgya sa bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin gyi rlabs kyi yul dang mangs/
15b1(phal chen): dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang /sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin lngas sgrub po//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan kyang sems
15b2(phal chen): can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/zhing la dmigs par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams lnga sangs rgyas
15b3(phal chen): kyi phrin las sgrub po//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang /sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub
15b4(phal chen): po/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsung par bzhugs pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub ste/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu
15b5(phal chen): po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub pa'o////bam po drug cu rtsa bzhi pa//kyi
15b6(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos te/bcu gang zhe na/smon lam chen po la rab tu
15b7(phal chen): brtan zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung pa de ltar mdzad cing gnyi su mi gsung ba 'di ni/sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dang po'o//phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug
16a1(phal chen): /pa'i sbrul b+h+yam+b+ha s+yA ng+ga du/ b+h+ya zlab sgom sang pa'i slong la smon tan m+b+has /sus pad+mam+b+ha p+na r+yA r+b+ba btsun da sprid lhag pa myi mdu' ga
16a2(phal chen): /sems can g+ha~M gan+d+ha pa'i chos gnyis pa'o//sems chena'i ma bar 'byu TIg ga cig gtsigs myed ga rten gyi khams brjod du me pa'i yang badza du med pang
16a3(phal chen): gshegs shing /rgyu ni khams rnams sa dru gshegs pa la thugs thegs pa /sems can ci sagasus du na//ni pa'i se sa rnams
16a4(phal chen): rmugs rkyen pas sgyums pa d+ma/dang 'i sems mas rmugs rkye ni ba sa rnams gyu na/mas can hUM hU~M/gdage na
16a5(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i byu chu N+DI yang dge par zhugs na mi blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byung rgyub mngon par sangs rgyas kyi bar du bzhin gshegs pa
16a6(phal chen): brnam pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ra ng+ge/d+hI chu kyi snyoms skye rnams 'i nA~M/sems pan / ba'i chos m+b+hi 'aM//dge ba
16a7(phal chen): thams cad yang dag par smra ci rnams pa ma byin pa nyid hU~M m+me rdza sa na kau/'jig rten pa'i rmyi la ma yin du 'di na/sems pa myo 'i chos drugs /
16b1(phal chen): ng+yas rgyas thams cad kyi rdza su spyon/sangs rgyas kyis spyad pa'i sem su lus kyi las dang /ngag go ltas dang /yod kyi las kyis slob cing nyan thos dang /rang sangs rgyas
16b2(phal chen): kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo ba med pos/bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni/sems can gyi gtso
16b3(phal chen): bo'i chos bdun pa'o//byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag tsing+ga/'od gsol la dngos pa/mas cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba/sangs rgyas kyi chos
16b4(phal chen): thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongasu rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni/sems can gyi gtso ba'i chos brgyud pa'o//'jig rten pa'i
16b5(phal chen): bde pa thams cing yongasu spangs te/'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang /'jig rten thams ca kyis gros pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad du mnyam pa
16b6(phal chen): nyid kyis 'jig rten thaMd bde bzed dang ldan par byas te/sdug bsngal dang /spros pa thams cad rab tu 'jom pa 'di ni/sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o//sdug
16b7(phal chen): bsngal gyi mi bde ba thams cad nyam su bab ste/'gro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub kyis shin tu gdungs kyang bla bar sems bskyed pas/sangs rgyas thams cad
17a1(phal chen): shA/rigs yongs su bsrung ba dang ldan pa dang /stobs bcu'i sa'i bar du/sangs rgyas kyi yul la myos pas mthar thug pa 'di ni/sems can gyi glatso/
17a2(phal chen): bo'i chos bcu pa ste/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dra dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di
17a3(phal chen): drug n+thi/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams ste/bcu gang zhe na/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
17a4(phal chen): ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/'jig///
17a5(phal chen): rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na bzhugs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams//
17a6(phal chen): thams cad na bzhugs pa dang /bzhengs pa dang /bzhud pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/'jig//
17a7(phal chen): rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus
17b1(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas nu bzhugs kyang /chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus
17b2(phal chen): pu thams cad kyi sngon gyis tha' dang /phyi ma'i mtha' dang /da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams

26a3(phal chen): ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la'ang rab tu mkhyen pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thob pa mkhas pa gnyis pa'o//

27a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par sgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom

39b1(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las dgu pa'o//de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya dran las 'da' ba'i tshe/'jig rten thams cad na sems can rnams sgro sngags 'don cing ngu bya

39b3(phal chen): pa thugs brtse ba can zhe 'am/lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad kyi skyabasu gyur pa/mgon du gyur pa/rten du gyur pa/bla na med pa bsod nams kyi
39b4(phal chen): zhing nub par gyur to zhe 'am/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'byung bar dka'o zhes rnam pa de lta bur smre sngags 'don pa dang /mya ngan byed pa dang /sangs rgyas mthong ba rjesu
39b5(phal chen): dran pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang /yid la bya ba de dang de dag gi sgo ra/sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad me da pa rgyun mi 'chad do//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yongasu mya
39b6(phal chen): ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/'di lta ste/sems can rnams kyi sems dad par bya ba'i dbang dang /sems can rnams dang pas mchod par bya ba'i dbang dang /sems can rnams lhag pa'i
39b7(phal chen): bsam pa rnam par sbyong bar bya ba'i dbang dang /sems can rnams yongasu smin par bya ba'i dbang dang /sems can rnams yongs su sbyang bar bya ba'i dbang dang /sems can rnams 'dul ba'i
40a1(phal chen): dbang sems can rnams bsod nams kyi tshogs yong su rdzogs par bya ba'i dbang dang /sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod bla
40a2(phal chen): dmigs par bya ba'i dbang dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten dam pa sna tshogasu brgyan pas/phyogs dang yul sna tshogasu sen rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags par bya ba'i
40a3(phal chen): dbang gis sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang /mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang /ring bsrel byin gyis rlobs te/lha dang klu dang /gnod sbyin dang /dri za dang /lha ma
40a4(phal chen): yin dang na mkha' lding dang /mi 'am ci dang /lto 'phye chen po dang /mi'i gnas thams cad du 'dul ba dang /mos pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang /ring bsrel byin
40a5(phal chen): gyis rlob bo//rang gi sku rnam par phye ste/sku gdung dang ring bsrel tshad med pa grangs med pa/dpag tu med pa/bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa
40a6(phal chen): gyis rlob po//de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten gyis sa nges rgyas kyi sku gdung 'jig rten thams cad du rnam par phye ba de'i yul dang /phyogs kyi klu'i gnas dang /
40a7(phal chen): gnod sbyin dang /dri za dang /lha ma yin dang /na mkha' lding dang /mi 'am tso dang /lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang /mi'i gnas dang /srin po'i gnas dag tu/sku gdung
40b1(phal chen): dang ring bsel mchod pa byed par 'gyur bas/sku gdung gi ring bsrel dang /dbu dang phyag sen gyi mchod rten dang /sangs rgyas bzhugs pa'i mchod rten la 'gro ba thams cad nges par
40b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas dran par 'gyur te/chos la rab tu rten par 'gyuraro//dge 'dun la dad pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyuraro//yul dang phyogs kyi gnas de dang de dag tu'ang rgyun mi 'chad par
40b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas mchod pa la brtson pa'i bsam pas sbyin pa yongasu gtong bar 'gyur ro//bsod nams byed par 'gyur ro//mtho ris de dang de yongasu dag pa rab tu 'thab par 'gyuraro//
40b4(phal chen): rigs dang rgyud kyi bdag nyid tsha ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro//longs spyod chen po dang 'khor rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyuraro//lha dang ma'i phun sum
40b5(phal chen): tshogs pa nyam su myong bar 'gyur ro//log par ltung ba med pa'i lam yongasu rdzogs par 'gyur ro//sangs rgyas 'byung ba don yod pa rab tu sgrub par 'gyur ro//chos
40b6(phal chen): dkar po la gnas pa yongasu rdzogs par byed par 'gyuraro//khams gsum pa las 'byung ba'i lam yongasu sbyong bar 'gyuraro//theg pa gang la dad pa'i smon gyis nges par 'byung
40b7(phal chen): bar 'gyur ro//de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag la drin du gzo ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la brten pa
41a1(phal chen): skyabs btsal ba dang /mgon btsal ba dang /dpung gnyen btsal ba'i sems bskyed par 'gyur ro//de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
41a2(phal chen): yongs su mya ngan laso 'das kyang yon bsam gyis mi khyab pa spyod ba/bsod nams zad mi shes pa'i yon gyi gnas drug ste/sang so rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
41a3(phal chen): 'jig rten du byung na/de ltar sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam pa mang po rab tu bsags pas bsod nams kyi tshogs rab tu rdzogs par 'gyur te/'di ni sangs
41a4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bcu pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
41a5(phal chen): rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so//de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs ma gtags par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis tshad gzung bar mi nus pa'o//
41a6(phal chen): 'das pa dang /ma 'ongs pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang /mangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs
41a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis med par spyod cing /dngos po rnam pa gnyis med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/sangs rgyas
41b1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/lung bstan pa thams cad ston pa la gnyis med par spyad do//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/snrums can sangs rgyas kyi rjesu dran pa la
41b2(phal chen): brtson pa rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa brjod du med pa 'byem klas pa rnams la gnyi su med par spyod do//sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi don ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas
41b3(phal chen): pas gnyis med pa'i sku rnam par dmigs par mdzad do//'das pa dang /mabyon pa dang /de ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rlung bzhin gnyis med par thugs
41b4(phal chen): chu pa mnga' ba'o//'byung ba dang /'byung ba'i mtha' gnyi su med pa dang /sngon gyi mtha' dang /phyi mo'i mtha' dang /da ltar byung ba'i mtha' gnyi su med par thugs su chud pa
41b5(phal chen): mnga' ba'o//sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gnyis su med pas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gcig par rab tu mkhyen cing ston pa zug su chud par mnga' ba'o//sangs
41b6(phal chen): rgyurgyas gci ba da /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gnyi su med par thugs chud pa mnga' ba'o//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis thug su chud pa dang /'dul ba mdzad
41b7(phal chen): po'i rnam par dmigs pa gnyis med par thug su chud pa mnga' ba'o//'jig rten gyi chos thams cad/sangs rgyas kyi chos gnyi su med par thug su chud pa mnga' ba'o//'das pa dang
42a1(phal chen): m+b+ha byon pa dang /de ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig ste/gnyis su med par thugasasu chud par myung
42a2(phal chen): 'o// rgyal po'o sgras ban+d+ha pA de da na/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams myi gnyis su med par spyod cing /dngos po gnyi su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gachaso//
42a3(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa/chos thams cad la rab tu bzhugs pa rnam so//bcu
42a4(phal chen): gang zhe na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i ye shes thug su chud pa lnga bzhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs
42a5(phal chen): rje chen po mi nyam po la bzhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam dzi lta ba bzhin du 'byung ba la bzhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
42a6(phal chen): rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can yongasu mi gtong bra la bzhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po med pa la gnas pa'i chos nyid la bzhugs
42a7(phal chen): po'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku skal pa mnyam pa the med cing don yod pa la bzhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
42b1(phal chen): rnams ni rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i thugs la bzhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad nyams pa med par gal ba la bzhugs pa'o///
42b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i thugs kyis rnam par spyod pa la bezhugs pa'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi mnyam
42b3(phal chen): pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha'i mtshan nyid la bzhugs pa ste/kye rgyal ba'i sgras bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
42b4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos thams cad la bzhugs pa rnamasaso//kye rgyal ba'i sgras bcu po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams
42b5(phal chen): cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa rnams te/bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'das pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon
42b6(phal chen): pA ra mkhyen pa dang /ma 'ongs pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /da ltar byung ba 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /
42b7(phal chen): tshig gi lam mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /'jig rten gyi rgyud mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /sems can gyi bsam pa dang /
43a1(phal chen): shes pa mtha dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu dang /'bring dang /chen po dang /rnam pa sna tshogs
43a2(phal chen): rnam par gnas pa'i mtshan nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la bsam pa tshad med pa yongasu mi btang bas/as rgyas kyi ye shes 'bar bar bya ba dang /yong su rdzogs par bya
43a3(phal chen): mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /chos thams cad 'tshang rgya ba'i mkhyen pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /'jig rten gyi rgyud thams cad rnam par dbye ba'i
43a4(phal chen): ye shes gzigs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /chos kyi dbyings kyi gon myig 'phrul gyi rnam pa lta bur dbye ba thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa ste/kye rgyal ba'i sas
43a5(phal chen): bcu po de dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad mo lus par mngon par mkhyen pa'o///bam po drug cu rtsa drug pa/kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu
43a6(phal chen): po 'di dag ni/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs chen po/stobs dam pa/stobs tshad med pa/stobs bdag nyid che sa/stobs thub pa med pa/stobs mi
43a7(phal chen): nyam pa/stobs snying po dang ldan pa/stobs mi shig pa/stobs 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa/stobs sems can thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa/
43b1(phal chen): sangang+yas rgyas kyi rgyal mtshan stobs blo che dpa' bo chen po'i stobs ste/bcu grang na na/'di lta ste/sangs rgyas kyi sku ni pha ral kyi gnad pa thams cad kyis mi shIgs mi chod pa'o//'jig
43b2(phal chen): rten gyi yul thams cad kyis sku tshe'i dbang po nyams par mi nus pa'o//'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi bskal pa'i me'i gdung bas 'tshig par mi nus pa'o//'jig rten gyi khams
43b3(phal chen): thams cad 'jig par gtogs pa'i chu'i phung por 'grongs par mi 'gyur ba'o//bdud thams cad dang /bdud kyi sde thams cad dang /lha thams cad kyi dpung dang /klu dang gnod sbyin
43b4(phal chen): dang /dri za dang lha ma yin dang /na mkha' lding dang /mi 'am ci dang /lto 'phye chen po dang /mri dang mI ma yin pa thams cad kyi dpung dang /sha za dang /srin po thams cad kyi
43b5(phal chen): dpung dang /sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi dpung gris brgal bar dka' dri'o//rdo rje ri rab kyi ri tsam gyi chur pa dang /khror yug gri ri chen po tsam dang /stong gsum gyi stong chen
43b6(phal chen): po tsam gyi rdo rje'i char bab kyang /bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ba sku gcig kyang 'gul bar mi 'gyur/g.yo bar
43b7(phal chen): mi 'gyur te/bag tsha ba'i shas mi mnga' ba'o//bzhugs sam/bzhengs sam/bzhud dam/gzims kyang rung ste/spyod lam 'gyur ba med do//de bzhin gshegs pa
44a1(phal chen): gdan bzhugs pa'i yul de dang /de'i khor dag tu yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes na kun tu 'bab par mi 'gyur ro//sangs rgyas kyi zhabs 'bring rnams
44a2(phal chen): la yang gnod par mi 'gyur ro//sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i sems can rnams la yang gnod par mi 'gyur zhing mi ga yon/de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku lta la smos
44a3(phal chen): kyang ci dgos te/'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dang po'o//gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom
44a4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams dgyes na/chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams ci rab kyi ri dang bcas pa/khor yug dang khor yug chen po'i ri drang ba
44a5(phal chen): pa/rgya mtsho dang ri drang nags tshul thibs po dang /sems can gnas pa'i gnas tha dad pa kun dang bcas pa/de lta bu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin
44a6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig tu btsud de/phyi ma'i mtha'i bskulbu pa'i mur thug par bzhag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par sems
44a7(phal chen): can rnams kyis shes par mi nus so//de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ni de snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams sku'i ba spu'i khung bu gcig gis bzung ste/phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i
44b1(phal chen): mur thugs par bsnams shing /gshegs sam/bzhugs snyam/bzhengs sam/gzims kyang rung ste/de bzhin gshegs bu'i thugs skad cig tsam+ba yang skyo
44b2(phal chen): bA mi mnga'o//chad cing dub par mi 'gyur ro//mthu dang stobs lnga yongs su nyam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o//spyod lam rnam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras
44b3(phal chen): 'di lta ste dper na/nA mkha' ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dzin kyang skyo ba med do//dub par med do//gnod pa med do//med par mi
44b4(phal chen): 'gyur ro//mi g.yo mi 'byung /mi 'jig go/de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang ba spu'i khung bu gcig du 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad bsnams
44b5(phal chen): kyang de'i rgyus thugs skad cig tsam du yang mi bde ba'i sku nyams mi 'byung ste/'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/sangs rgyas kyi spyod
44b6(phal chen): pa'i rgyal ma tshan gyi chos gnyis pa'o//gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams go shegs stabs gtsug tu bzhud pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med po'i yang
44b7(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams yongasu 'da' zhing thugs bskyed pa gcig gis bsgral pa tha dad pa'i rim pa/sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang
45a1(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i rdul shon ta phra ba skrod 'byung ngur mdzad//de lta bur ga shogs pas bskal pa 'jog rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu pra ba snyed
45a2(phal chen): drug shegs shing jig na gyi khams thams cad kyi snangs kyi rgyud ni skyed pa'i/lA par bdud de/'jig ts+tsha khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu za bskyed
45a3(phal chen): kyi 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du 'khor kun tu rgya che zhing yangs pa'i 'khor yu ga chen po'i rdo rje'i ri dang /sangs rgyas kyi zhing gre rnam pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la
45a4(phal chen): bsgres pa snyed kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang de la bsgres pa de snyed pa spu'i khung bu gcig tu btsud de/ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu ji lta ba bzhin du sku'i ba spu'i khung bu thaMd du btsud/
45a5(phal chen): ba spu'i khung bu yang sems can thams cad snyed du gyur la de dag thams cad bsnams te/de snyed kyi ba spu'i khung bur tshul de bzhin du bshams te/thugs bskyed pa
45a6(phal chen): de lta bus de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyu zhing gi shegs sam/phyogs kyi dra ba thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/na mkha'i
45a7(phal chen): dbyings thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud 'grangs pa sngon gyi mthar gtogs pa nas bzung spro/phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug
45b1(phal chen): bang de bzhin dug shogs pas bskal bya thams cad dad par gyur kyang de bzhin gshegs pa bzhud pa lnga brtson pa ni nyams par mi 'gyur ro//sku nyam chung bur mi 'gyur ro//
45b2(phal chen): thugs rnam par 'khrug par mi 'gyuraro//ting nge 'dzin nyams par mi 'gyur ro//de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yongasu nyams par mi 'gyur//'di ni sangs rgyas
45b3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gsum pa'o//gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
45b4(phal chen): ni bsod snyoms gcig bzhes nas bskal pra brjod du med par dkyil mo krung gcig bcas pas nyin mtshan gyi rgyud du sngon gyi mtha' dang /phyi ma'i mtha'i mur gtogs pa'i
45b5(phal chen): bskal pa 'das par bzhugs kyang sku mi g.yo zhing bde ba'i dam pa la spyod pa dang /sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas/rnam par spyod kyang
45b6(phal chen): sems can 'ga' tsam la'ang /sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro//de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yong su bkod//
45b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gcig gi lus kyang 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra bsnyed tsam du che ba
46a1(phal chen): de lta bur gyur la/sems can gcig gi lus kyi tshad ji tsam pa de tsam gyi lus su sems can thams cad kyang gyur la/sems can de dgar ra/
46a2(phal chen): gzugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi lcing ji tsam yod pa de tsam du gyur te/sems can gcig ji ltar lci ba bzhin du sems can thams cad re re'i lcid kyang
46a3(phal chen): de tsam du 'gyur te/sems can de dag thams cad nga bzhin gshegs pa'i phyog sor gyi rtse mo gcig la phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal po'i mur thug par bsnams te/phyag sor
46a4(phal chen): gyi rtse mo gcig gis ji ltar bsnams pa de bzhin du phyag sor thams cad kyi rtse mo la'ang de tsam re re bsnams kyang /de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa la sku mnyal ba 'am//thug
46a5(phal chen): dub par mi 'gyur te thugs bskyed pa'i cha shas shin tu phra ba gcig tsam du yang sdug bsngal mi bde ba skye bar mi 'gyur ro//de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa dang /na mkha'i
46a6(phal chen): dbyangs la 'jug pa dang /phyogs kyi dra ba'i rnam pa la 'jug pa re re dang /de lta bu le 'jug pa/nam mkha'i khams ma lus pa'i dbyings kyis klas pa/chos kyi dbyings kyi mnya
46a7(phal chen): gtugs pa/skra'i rtse mo'i chi shas kyis gzhal nga'i 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa thams cad re re zhing yang /skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal te/na mkha'i dbyings kyi kun tu//
46b1(phal chen): mas das smras rdzun na rgyu ga nams ga t+ta/da ga shan pa pa sung sgrub du/sam+ba nga //
46b2(phal chen): gocig tu bzhugs pa'i spyang pas/na gyi mtha' dang /phyi ma ma dzu drug pam phrul pa zang po mdzad/bskal pa 'da' bar mdzod cing bskul pa la ni
46b3(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu ba che chen po'i stobs/sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o//gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'a
46b4(phal chen): rnams ni sku gcig lnga dbu sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod byed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs te//dbu re re la ljags sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i

105a2(phal chen): 'gro ba med//gang du 'gro ba de bzhin ma migs so//rgyu mtshad med yin te//sgyu mched kyis dmigs par bya ba'ang ma yin no//tshad med tshed dang ldan pa yang //chog
105a3(phal chen): kyi dbus su ston pa rab tu byed//de bzhin rtogs pa'i blo ldan pa//sangs rgyas kun gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams las byung //sems ni tshad yod ma yin te//tshad med pa la
105a4(phal chen): gnas pa'ang de dag min//'du shes rnam pa gcig min te//de dag chad med pa dang tshod dang ldan pa ston//lam gyi rgyud dang 'brel ba med//tshad med rnams gnas pa'ang de bzhin med//sangs

105b2(phal chen): mkhas//sems can bgrang tshul shes kyang grangs la skyes pa med//chos kyi sprin chen char 'bebs shing //'jig rten khams rnams thams cad snang bar byed//sangs rgyas

105b5(phal chen): bskal pa rnams dang zhing la pha rol phyin pa thob//phyogs rnams rgya mtsho gangs chen mchor//ye shes rgya mtsho'i tshul la mkhas pas zhugs//lus rnams thams ni
105b6(phal chen): las/sems can kun gyi lus rnams sna tshogs ji snyed dang //sangs rgyas spya mtha' las pa//ye shes shin tu yangs pa de ston te//skad cig gcig gi dus tshul la/
105b7(phal chen): mi'i gtso bo mang po 'byung ba rab tu shes//bskal pa mang po brjod ming du//mi yi seng lce bgrang bas zad mi 'gyur//de dag mya ngan 'da' ba yang //skad cig gcig la
106a1(phal chen): med shin tu yangs pa 'byung //rnying bsil rnam dbye mang po yang //ye shes d+hI med phra bas ston pa byed//de bzhin ma 'ongs dus kyi yang //mi'i seng ge mtha'
106a2(phal chen): yas smon lam 'debs pa'i rnams//byang chub dri med sems bskyod pa//ye shes yangs shing shin tu phra bas shos//bzang po spyod la gnas bcas shing //de bzhin dus
106a3(phal chen): gsum gshegs pa'i sems can gtso bo rnams//ji snyed skyes por gyur pa dag/de dag thams cad ma lus rab tu shes//de ltar rab tu shes pas na//mtha' dang dpung
106a4(phal chen): mr-ing spyod pa'i sa dang de bzhin du//ye shes 'byung gnas blo gros la//ye shes 'khor lo'i spyod pas phyir mi ldog/ye shes phra mo rab yangs pa//stobs bcu rnams
106a5(phal chen): kyi spyod yul mchog la de dag zhugs//bzang po rtogs pa'i blo can rnams//phyir mi ldog la 'jug pa brjod bya na//sangs rgyas rgyal ba thams cad kyi//yang dag gzhol

106b1(phal chen): mi slosgrub sems kyang de bzhin rab tu shes//sems rgyud de dag re re la yang //sems rnams brjod du med pa mngon 'tshang rgyu//gcig dang gnyis su shes pa med//de dag yongs
106b2(phal chen): 'dres par 'gyur ba'ang med pa ste//so so'i 'du shi sa rnam pa la//sems can de dag skyes par gyur pa yin//'di ni 'dug par mthor gyur kyang //sems can brjod med gzhan
106b3(phal chen): dang gzhan sems ldan pa'i rnams//gzhan gyi zhing phyi na 'du shes kyang //'jig rten sna tshogs rnams la rab tu skye//'di 'dra'i tshul la 'jug pa la//spyod pa'i mchog gis
106b4(phal chen): rjes su zhugs par gyur pa'i rnams//kun+da tu bzang po'i ming thob ste//'jig rten mgon po kun gyi rjes su skyes//sems can bye ba la la ni//ngan song 'grongs pa'i ming tham/

107b1(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid tshul gyus//sangs rgyus yA shes kun tu mtha' yang yas////shin tu rgyas pa tshon pa'i mdo//sangs rgyas phal pa che zhes bya ba las

107b3(phal chen): pa'i thugs mnga' ba/'das pa dang /ma byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang /sku gcig pas mnyam pa nyid brnyes pa/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi

107b6(phal chen): yul la shin tu dgyes pa/chos kyi sku na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas klas pa mnga' ba/de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi pho brang khang pa d+ma rtsigs pa'i gzhal
